POR_alliance_game = {
	icon = GFX_decision_category_foreign_policy

	allowed = {
		original_tag = POR
	}

	visible = { 

	}
    POR_establish_rk_TUN = {
	icon = generic_prepare_civil_war

		highlight_states = {
			highlight_state_targets = {
				state = 273
				state = 1009
				state = 514
				state = 448
				state = 450
				state = 451
				state = 805
				state = 665
				state = 663
				state = 458
				state = 459
				state = 460
				state = 513
			}
			highlight_color_while_active = 3
			highlight_color_before_active = 2
		}

	available = {
		273 = { owner = { OR = { original_tag = POR is_subject_of = POR } } }
		1009 = { owner = { OR = { original_tag = POR is_subject_of = POR } } }
		514 = { owner = { OR = { original_tag = POR is_subject_of = POR } } }
		448 = { owner = { OR = { original_tag = POR is_subject_of = POR } } }
		450 = { owner = { OR = { original_tag = POR is_subject_of = POR } } }
		451 = { owner = { OR = { original_tag = POR is_subject_of = POR } } }
		805 = { owner = { OR = { original_tag = POR is_subject_of = POR } } }
		665 = { owner = { OR = { original_tag = POR is_subject_of = POR } } }
		663 = { owner = { OR = { original_tag = POR is_subject_of = POR } } }
		458 = { owner = { OR = { original_tag = POR is_subject_of = POR } } }
		459 = { owner = { OR = { original_tag = POR is_subject_of = POR } } }
		460 = { owner = { OR = { original_tag = POR is_subject_of = POR } } }
		513 = { owner = { OR = { original_tag = POR is_subject_of = POR } } }
	}

	fire_only_once = yes

	ai_will_do = {
		factor = 5
	}
	complete_effect = {
		TUN = {
			every_core_state = {
				remove_core_of = TUN
			}
		}
		273 = { add_core_of = TUN }
		1009 = { add_core_of = TUN }
		514 = { add_core_of = TUN }
		448 = { add_core_of = TUN }
		450 = { add_core_of = TUN }
		451 = { add_core_of = TUN }
		805 = { add_core_of = TUN }
		665 = { add_core_of = TUN }
		663 = { add_core_of = TUN }
		458 = { add_core_of = TUN }
		459 = { add_core_of = TUN }
		460 = { add_core_of = TUN }
		513 = { add_core_of = TUN }
		release = TUN
		TUN = { 
			every_core_state = {
				limit = {
					AND = {
						NOT = { 
							is_core_of = POR
						}
						OR = {
							is_owned_by = POR
							OWNER = { is_subject_of = POR} 
						}
					}
				}
				transfer_state_to = TUN
			}
		}
		TUN = { 
			set_cosmetic_tag = POR_TUN_OCC
			load_focus_tree = generic_focus            

			create_country_leader = {
				name = "Portuguese Administration"
				picture = "gfx/leaders/WDPOR/portugal_colonial_administration.png"
				expire = "1.1.1"
				ideology = integralism_subtype
				traits = {
				}
			}

			set_popularities = {
				syndicalist = 5.0
				social_democrat = 5.0
				social_liberal = 0.0
				market_liberal = 0.0
				social_conservative = 20.0
				authoritarian_democrat = 50.0
				paternal_autocrat = 10.0
				national_populist = 10.0
			}
			set_party_name = {
				ideology = paternal_autocrat
				name = "Portuguese Administration"
				long_name = "Portuguese Administration"
			}
			set_party_name = {
				ideology = national_populist
				name = "Portuguese Administration"
				long_name = "Portuguese Administration"
			}

			POR = {
				set_autonomy = {
					target = TUN
					autonomous_state = kx_colored_puppet
				}
			}

			set_politics = {
				ruling_party = national_populist
				elections_allowed = no
			}
		}
	}
}

POR_establish_rk_WAL = {
	icon = generic_prepare_civil_war

		highlight_states = {
			highlight_state_targets = {
				state = 122
				state = 1225
			}
			highlight_color_while_active = 3
			highlight_color_before_active = 2
		}

	available = {
		122 = { owner = { OR = { original_tag = POR is_subject_of = POR } } }
		1225 = { owner = { OR = { original_tag = POR is_subject_of = POR } } }
	}

	fire_only_once = yes

	ai_will_do = {
		factor = 5
	}
	complete_effect = {
		WAL = {
			every_core_state = {
				remove_core_of = WAL
			}
		}
		122 = { add_core_of = WAL }
		1225 = { add_core_of = WAL }
		release = WAL
		WAL = { 
			every_core_state = {
				limit = {
					AND = {
						NOT = { 
							is_core_of = POR
						}
						OR = {
							is_owned_by = POR
							OWNER = { is_subject_of = POR} 
						}
					}
				}
				transfer_state_to = WAL
			}
		}
		WAL = { 
			set_cosmetic_tag = POR_WAL_OCC
			load_focus_tree = generic_focus            

			create_country_leader = {
				name = "Portuguese Administration"
				picture = "gfx/leaders/WDPOR/portugal_colonial_administration.png"
				expire = "1.1.1"
				ideology = integralism_subtype
				traits = {
				}
			}

			set_popularities = {
				syndicalist = 5.0
				social_democrat = 5.0
				social_liberal = 0.0
				market_liberal = 0.0
				social_conservative = 20.0
				authoritarian_democrat = 50.0
				paternal_autocrat = 10.0
				national_populist = 10.0
			}
			set_party_name = {
				ideology = paternal_autocrat
				name = "Portuguese Administration"
				long_name = "Portuguese Administration"
			}
			set_party_name = {
				ideology = national_populist
				name = "Portuguese Administration"
				long_name = "Portuguese Administration"
			}

			POR = {
				set_autonomy = {
					target = WAL
					autonomous_state = kx_colored_puppet
				}
			}

			set_politics = {
				ruling_party = national_populist
				elections_allowed = no
			}
		}
	}
}
